<![endif]--> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Highest Teachings in Instructions<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Divine Life Society Publication: </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.sivanandaonline.org/public_html/?cmd=displaysection&amp;section_id=649&amp;parent=632&amp;format=html"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Yoga of Synthesis</b></span></a></span><b> by Sri Swami <a name="_VPID_65">Sivananda<o:p></o:p></a></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">1. Reduce your wants to the utmost minimum.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 2. Adapt yourself to circumstances.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 3. Never be attached to anything or anybody.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 4. Share what you have with others.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 5. Be ever ready to serve. Lose no opportunity. Serve with Atma Bhava.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 6. Entertain Akarta and Sakshi Bhava.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 7. Speak measured and sweet words.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 8. Have a burning thirst for God-realisation.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 9. Renounce all your belongings and surrender yourself unto God.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 10. Spiritual path is a sharp-edged razor path. A Guru is absolutely necessary.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 11. Have great patience and perseverance.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 12. Never leave the Abhyasa even for a day.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 13. The Guru will only guide you. You should yourself tread the path.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 14. Life is short. Time of death is uncertain. Apply yourself seriously to Yogic Sadhana.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 15. Maintain daily spiritual diary and record correctly your progress and failures. Stick to resolves.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 16. Do not complain that there is no time for Sadhana. Reduce sleep and tall talks. Stick to Brahmamuhurta.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 17. Let the thought of God (Reality) keep away the thought of the world.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 18. Forget the feeling that you are so and so-a male or a female-by vigorous Brahma Chintana.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 19. Never postpone a thing for tomorrow if it is possible for you to do it today.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 20. Do not boast or make a show of your abilities. Be simple and humble.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 21. Be cheerful always. Give up worries.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 22. Be indifferent to things that do not concern you.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 23. Fly away from company and discussion.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 24. Be alone for a few hours daily.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 25. Give up greediness, jealousy and hoarding.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 26. Control your emotions by discrimination and Vairagya.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 27. Maintain equilibrium of mind always.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 28. Think twice before you speak and thrice before you act.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 29. Give up back-biting, criticising and fault-finding. Beware of reaction.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 30. Find out your own faults and weaknesses. See only good in others. Praise the virtues of others.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 31. Forgive and forget the harm done by others. Do good to those who hate you.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 32. Shun lust, anger, egoism, Moha and Lobha like a venomous cobra.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 33. Be prepared to suffer any amount of pain.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 34. Have a set of maxims always with you to induce Vairagya.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 35. Treat sensual enjoyment as poison, vomited food, Vishta or urine. They cannot give you satisfaction.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 36. Preserve your Virya carefully. Sleep always separately.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 37. Revere ladies as Mother Divine. Prostrate before all.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 38. See God in every face, in everything.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 39. Take to Sankirtan, Satsanga, prayer, when the mind is overpowered by lower instincts.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 40. Face obstacles coolly and boldly.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 41. Care not for criticism when you are in the right path. Yield not to flattery.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 42. Respect rogues and scoundrels. Serve them.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 43. Admit your faults plainly.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 44. Take care of your health. Do not neglect daily Asanas and exercises.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 45. Be active and nimble always.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 46. Develop your heart by giving. Be extraordinarily charitable. Give more than one's expectations.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 47. Desires multiply misery. Develop contentment.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 48. Control the senses one by one.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 49. Develop Brahmakara Vritti by repeated thinking.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 50. Have a check over all your thoughts. Keep them pure and sublime.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 51. Do not lose temper when anybody insults, taunts or rebukes you. It is a mere play of words and a variety of sounds.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 52. Rest your mind in God and live in Truth.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 53. Be up and doing in the path of perfection.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 54. Have a definite aim in your life and proceed cautiously.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 55. Benefits of Mouna are incalculable. Never give up this practice.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 56. Four important means for passion to enter the mind are sound, touch, sight and thoughts. Be vigilant!</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 57. Have intimate connection with none but God. Mix little with others.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 58. Be moderate in everything. Extremes are always dangerous.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 59. Every day have self-analysis and introspection. Know the amount of your growth.</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> 60. Give up curiosities in spiritual path. Conserve your energy and concentrate. Think little of food, body and relatives. Think more of Atman. You must realise in this very birth itself!</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b>Excerpts from: </b></span><b>Highest Teachings in Instructions - </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.sivanandaonline.org/public_html/?cmd=displaysection&amp;section_id=649&amp;parent=632&amp;format=html"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Yoga of Synthesis</b></span></a></span></span><b><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
